Loading theory "Draft.Templates" (required by "Draft.ProgressMoreTemplates" via "Draft.ExtrEqs")
datatype template_term
=
     t_empty
   | template_app of template_term * template_term
   | template_hole of int
   | template_var of int
datatype sign
= equals | greater_equals | greater_than | less_equals | less_than
datatype template
=
     template_bimplication of template * template
   | template_dunno
   | template_equation of template_term * template_term
   | template_implication of template list * template
   | template_inequation of sign * template_term * template_term
   | template_negation of template
   | template_predicate of template_term
constructor t_empty: template_term
constructor template_app: template_term * template_term -> template_term
constructor template_hole: int -> template_term
constructor template_var: int -> template_term
constructor equals: sign
constructor greater_equals: sign
constructor greater_than: sign
constructor less_equals: sign
constructor less_than: sign
constructor template_bimplication: template * template -> template
constructor template_dunno: template
constructor template_equation: template_term * template_term -> template
constructor template_implication: template list * template -> template
constructor template_inequation:
   sign * template_term * template_term -> template
constructor template_negation: template -> template
constructor template_predicate: template_term -> template

val indexOf = fn: ''a list -> ''a -> int -> int
val has_eq = fn: term -> bool

   (indexname * typ) list -> (string * typ) list -> term -> template_term
val lemma2predicate = fn: term -> term -> template
val makeTemplatewithContext = fn: term -> term -> template
val lemma2template = fn: term -> template
val thm2template = fn: thm -> template
val tterm2string = fn: template_term -> string
val template2string = fn: template -> string

    ("Progress.WTrt_inducts2",
     "[| ?P,?x1a,?h,?sh \<turnstile> ?x2a : ?x3a;
         !!C E. is_class ?P C ==> ?P1.0 E (new C) (Class C);
         !!E e T C.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : T; ?P1.0 E e T; is_refT T;
               is_class ?P C |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (Cast C e) (Class C);
         !!v T E.
            typeof\<^bsub>?h\<^esub> v = \<lfloor>T\<rfloor> ==>
            ?P1.0 E (Val v) T;
         !!E v T. E v = \<lfloor>T\<rfloor> ==> ?P1.0 E (Var v) T;
         !!E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 : T\<^sub>1;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E
                 (e\<^sub>1 \<guillemotleft>Eq\<guillemotright> e\<^sub>2)
                 Boolean;
         !!E e\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 : Integer;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 Integer;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : Integer;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 Integer |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E
                 (e\<^sub>1 \<guillemotleft>Add\<guillemotright> e\<^sub>2)
                 Integer;
         !!E V T e T'.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> Var V : T; ?P1.0 E (Var V) T;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : T'; ?P1.0 E e T';
               ?P \<turnstile> T' \<le> T |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (V:=e) Void;
         !!E e C F T D.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : Class C; ?P1.0 E e (Class C);
               ?P \<turnstile> C has F,NonStatic:T in D |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (e\<bullet>F{D}) T;
         !!E e F D T.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : NT; ?P1.0 E e NT |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (e\<bullet>F{D}) T;
         !!C F T D E.
            ?P \<turnstile> C has F,Static:T in D ==>
            ?P1.0 E (C\<bullet>\<^sub>sF{D}) T;
         !!E e\<^sub>1 C F T D e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 : Class C;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 (Class C);
               ?P \<turnstile> C has F,NonStatic:T in D;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>2 \<le> T |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (e\<^sub>1\<bullet>F{D} := e\<^sub>2) Void;
         !!E e\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 F D.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 : NT;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 NT;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (e\<^sub>1\<bullet>F{D} := e\<^sub>2) Void;
         !!C F T D E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2.
            [| ?P \<turnstile> C has F,Static:T in D;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>2 \<le> T |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (C\<bullet>\<^sub>sF{D} := e\<^sub>2) Void;
         !!E e C M Ts T pns body D es Ts'.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : Class C; ?P1.0 E e (Class C);
               ?P \<turnstile> C sees M, NonStatic :  Ts\<rightarrow>T = (pns,
                                    body) in D;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> es [:] Ts'; ?P2.0 E es Ts';
               ?P \<turnstile> Ts' [\<le>] Ts |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (e\<bullet>M(es)) T;
         !!E e es Ts M T.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : NT; ?P1.0 E e NT;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> es [:] Ts; ?P2.0 E es Ts |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (e\<bullet>M(es)) T;
         !!C M Ts T pns body D E es Ts' sfs vs.
            [| ?P \<turnstile> C sees M, Static :  Ts\<rightarrow>T = (pns,
                                 body) in D;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> es [:] Ts'; ?P2.0 E es Ts';
               ?P \<turnstile> Ts' [\<le>] Ts;
               M = clinit -->
               ?sh D = \<lfloor>(sfs, Processing)\<rfloor> &
               es = map Val vs |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (C\<bullet>\<^sub>sM(es)) T;
         !!E. ?P2.0 E [] [];
         !!E e T es Ts.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : T; ?P1.0 E e T;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> es [:] Ts; ?P2.0 E es Ts |]
            ==> ?P2.0 E (e # es) (T # Ts);
         !!v T\<^sub>1 T E V e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2.
            [| typeof\<^bsub>?h\<^esub> v = \<lfloor>T\<^sub>1\<rfloor>;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>1 \<le> T;
               ?P,E(V |-> T),?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 (E(V |-> T)) e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E {V:T; V:=Val v;; e\<^sub>2} T\<^sub>2;
         !!E V T e T'.
            [| ?P,E(V |-> T),?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : T';
               ?P1.0 (E(V |-> T)) e T'; ~ assigned V e |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E {V:T; e} T';
         !!E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 : T\<^sub>1;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (e\<^sub>1;; e\<^sub>2) T\<^sub>2;
         !!E e e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 T.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : Boolean; ?P1.0 E e Boolean;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 : T\<^sub>1;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>1 \<le> T\<^sub>2 |
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>2 \<le> T\<^sub>1;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>1 \<le> T\<^sub>2 --> T = T\<^sub>2;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>2 \<le> T\<^sub>1 -->
               T = T\<^sub>1 |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (if (e) e\<^sub>1 else e\<^sub>2) T;
         !!E e c T.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : Boolean; ?P1.0 E e Boolean;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> c : T; ?P1.0 E c T |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (while (e) c) Void;
         !!E e T\<^sub>r T.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : T\<^sub>r; ?P1.0 E e T\<^sub>r;
               is_refT T\<^sub>r |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (throw e) T;
         !!E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1 V C e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 : T\<^sub>1;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1;
               ?P,E(V |->
               Class C),?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 : T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 (E(V |-> Class C)) e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>1 \<le> T\<^sub>2 |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (try e\<^sub>1 catch(C V) e\<^sub>2) T\<^sub>2;
         !!E e T C Cs b.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : T; ?P1.0 E e T;
               ALL C':set (C # Cs). is_class ?P C'; ~ sub_RI e;
               ALL C':set (tl Cs).
                  EX sfs. ?sh C' = \<lfloor>(sfs, Processing)\<rfloor>;
               b -->

                   EX sfs. ?sh C' = \<lfloor>(sfs, Processing)\<rfloor>);
               distinct Cs; supercls_lst ?P Cs |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (INIT C (Cs,b) \<leftarrow> e) T;
         !!E e T e' T' C Cs.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : T; ?P1.0 E e T;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e' : T'; ?P1.0 E e' T';
               ALL C':set (C # Cs). is_class ?P C'; ~ sub_RI e';
               ALL C':set (C # Cs). not_init C' e;
               ALL C':set Cs.
                  EX sfs. ?sh C' = \<lfloor>(sfs, Processing)\<rfloor>;
               EX sfs.
                  ?sh C = \<lfloor>(sfs, Processing)\<rfloor> |
                  ?sh C = \<lfloor>(sfs, Error)\<rfloor> &
                  e = THROW NoClassDefFoundError;
               distinct (C # Cs); supercls_lst ?P (C # Cs) |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (RI (C,e) ; Cs \<leftarrow> e') T' |]
      ==> ?P1.0 ?x1a ?x2a ?x3a",

               distinct Cs; supercls_lst ?P Cs |]

         !!E e T e' T' C Cs.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e : T; ?P1.0 E e T;

               EX sfs.
                  ?sh C = \<lfloor>(sfs, Processing)\<rfloor> |
                  ?sh C = \<lfloor>(sfs, Error)\<rfloor> &
                  e = THROW NoClassDefFoundError;
               distinct (C # Cs); supercls_lst ?P (C # Cs) |]

     "[| ?P,?x1a,?h,?sh \<turnstile> ?x2a :' ?x3a;
         !!C E. is_class ?P C ==> ?P1.0 E (new C) (Class C);
         !!E e T C.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e :' T; ?P1.0 E e T; is_refT T;
               is_class ?P C |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E (Cast C e) (Class C);
         !!v T E.
            typeof\<^bsub>?h\<^esub> v = \<lfloor>T\<rfloor> ==>
            ?P1.0 E (Val v) T;
         !!E v T. E v = \<lfloor>T\<rfloor> ==> ?P1.0 E (Var v) T;
         !!E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 :' T\<^sub>1;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 :' T\<^sub>2;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E
                 (e\<^sub>1 \<guillemotleft>Eq\<guillemotright> e\<^sub>2)
                 Boolean;
         !!E e\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 :' Integer;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 Integer;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>2 :' Integer;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 Integer |]
            ==> ?P1.0 E
                 (e\<^sub>1 \<guillemotleft>Add\<guillemotright> e\<^sub>2)
                 Integer;
         !!E V T e T'.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> Var V :' T; ?P1.0 E (Var V) T;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e :' T'; ?P1.0 E e T';
               ?P \<turnstile> T' \<le> T |]

         !!E e C F T D.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e :' Class C; ?P1.0 E e (Class C);
               ?P \<turnstile> C has F,NonStatic:T in D |]

               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 (Class C);
               ?P \<turnstile> C has F,NonStatic:T in D;

               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>2 \<le> T |]

         !!E e\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 F D.

               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>2 \<le> T |]

         !!E e C M Ts T pns body D es Ts'.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e :' Class C; ?P1.0 E e (Class C);

                                    body) in D;

               ?P \<turnstile> Ts' [\<le>] Ts |]

         !!E e e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1 e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2 T.
            [| ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e :' Boolean; ?P1.0 E e Boolean;
               ?P,E,?h,?sh \<turnstile> e\<^sub>1 :' T\<^sub>1;
               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1;

               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>2 T\<^sub>2;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>1 \<le> T\<^sub>2 |
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>2 \<le> T\<^sub>1;
               ?P \<turnstile> T\<^sub>1 \<le> T\<^sub>2 --> T = T\<^sub>2;

               ?P1.0 E e\<^sub>1 T\<^sub>1;
